namespace = trigger_china_frontier_event

trigger_china_frontier_event.1 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		num_of_cities > 220
		NOT = {
			has_variable = off_real_mode
		}

	immediate = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = china_frontier.1

namespace = china_frontier
china_frontier.1 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.1.t"
	desc = "china_frontier.1.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier
	goto_location = scope:wuhuan_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					is_in_region = modong_region
					is_in_region = mobei_region
					is_in_region = you_region
				}
			}
		}
		area:wuhuan_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_wuhuan
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = wuhuan_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = wuhuan_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_wuhuan
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = wuhuan_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_wuhuan
			days = 9125
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = wuhuan_frontier_cost
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.c"		#維持50年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_wuhuan
			days = 18250
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = wuhuan_frontier_cost
			duration = 18250
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:wuhuan_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "WUH"
						adjective = "WUH_ADJ"
					}
					save_scope_as = wuhuan_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:8766.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_kingdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:wuhuan_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = wuhuan_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:wuhuan_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:wuhuan_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "WUH"
						adjective = "WUH_ADJ"
					}
					save_scope_as = wuhuan_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:8766.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_kingdom
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = wuhuan_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:wuhuan_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

china_frontier.2 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.2.t"
	desc = "china_frontier.2.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier
	goto_location = scope:yinshan_north_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					is_in_region = modong_region
					is_in_region = mobei_region
				}
			}
		}
		area:yinshan_north_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_yinshan_north
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = yinshan_north_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = yinshan_north_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_yinshan_north
			days = 3650
		}

			name = yinshan_north_frontier_cost

			multiply = -2.4
		}

					name = {
						name = "XNU"
						adjective = "XNU_ADJ"
					}
					save_scope_as = yinshan_north_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:9512.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:yinshan_north_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = yinshan_north_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:yinshan_north_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

				factor = 100

				}

		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:guyan_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "GYN"
						adjective = "GYN_ADJ"
					}
					save_scope_as = guyan_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:9483.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = guyan_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:guyan_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

china_frontier.9 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.9.t"
	desc = "china_frontier.9.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier
	goto_location = scope:gonglu_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					is_in_region = modong_region
					is_in_region = mobei_region
				}
			}
		}
		area:gonglu_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_gonglu
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = gonglu_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = gonglu_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_gonglu
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gonglu_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}

			multiply = -2.4
		}

			scope:darn_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "darn_area"
						adjective = "darn_area"
					}
					save_scope_as = darn_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:5879.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:darn_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = darn_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:darn_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:darn_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "darn_area"
						adjective = "darn_area"
					}
					save_scope_as = darn_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:5879.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = darn_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:darn_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

3china_frontier.21 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.21.t"	#桥畔斯基泰
	desc = "china_frontier.21.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier_steppe
	goto_location = scope:scythia_ad_pontem_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				is_in_region = scythia_region
			}
		}
		area:scythia_ad_pontem_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_scythia_ad_pontem
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = scythia_ad_pontem_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = scythia_ad_pontem_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_scythia_ad_pontem
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = scythia_ad_pontem_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_scythia_ad_pontem
			days = 9125
		}

			modifier = {

					}

			}
		}

			}

	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.31.t"	#辛迪卡
	desc = "china_frontier.31.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier_steppe
	goto_location = scope:alania_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				is_in_region = sarmatia_asiatica_region
			}
		}
		area:alania_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_alania
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = alania_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = alania_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_alania
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = alania_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_alania
			days = 9125
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = alania_frontier_cost
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.c"		#維持50年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_alania
			days = 18250
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = alania_frontier_cost
			duration = 18250
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:alania_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "SCE"
						adjective = "SCE"
					}
					save_scope_as = alania_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:7619.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:alania_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = alania_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:alania_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:alania_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "SCE"
						adjective = "SCE"
					}
					save_scope_as = alania_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:7619.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = alania_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:alania_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:bassetia_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = bassetia_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:bassetia_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:bassetia_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "bassetia_area"

					}

				is_in_region = vistulia_region
			}
		}
		area:vistulia_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {

		}
	}

		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = vistulia_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = vistulia_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_vistulia
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = vistulia_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}

6china_frontier.52 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.52.t"	#吕根
	desc = "china_frontier.52.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier_forest
	goto_location = scope:rugia_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				is_in_region = venedia_region
			}
		}
		area:rugia_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_rugia
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = rugia_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = rugia_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_rugia
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rugia_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_rugia
			days = 9125
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rugia_frontier_cost
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.c"		#維持50年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_rugia
			days = 18250
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rugia_frontier_cost
			duration = 18250
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:rugia_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "RGG"
						adjective = "RGG"
					}
					save_scope_as = rugia_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:4751.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:rugia_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = rugia_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:rugia_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:rugia_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "RGG"
						adjective = "RGG"
					}
					save_scope_as = rugia_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:4751.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = rugia_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:rugia_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

6china_frontier.53 = {
	type = country_event

				is_in_region = venedia_region

				owner = root
			}

					is_in_area = helveconia_area

			days = 3650
		}

			name = helveconia_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:helveconia_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "LGI"
						adjective = "LGI"
					}

					set_primary_culture = p:4758.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:helveconia_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = helveconia_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:helveconia_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

			}

	option = {

				}

			root = {

				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {

				}

			}
		}

7china_frontier.63 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.63.t"	#法罗得尼亚
	desc = "china_frontier.63.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier_forest
	goto_location = scope:pharodenia_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				is_in_region = germania_region
			}
		}
		area:pharodenia_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_pharodenia
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = pharodenia_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = pharodenia_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_pharodenia
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = pharodenia_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_pharodenia
			days = 9125
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = pharodenia_frontier_cost
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			days = 18250
		}

			duration = 18250
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:pharodenia_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "pharodenia_area"
						adjective = "pharodenia_area"
					}
					save_scope_as = pharodenia_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:3898.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_chiefdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:pharodenia_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = pharodenia_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:pharodenia_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:pharodenia_frontier = {

				}
				save_scope_as = east_gothia_frontier
			}
		}
	}

		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:taifa_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "TQF"
						adjective = "TQF"
					}
					save_scope_as = taifa_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:7576.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_kingdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:taifa_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = taifa_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:taifa_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:taifa_frontier = {

		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				is_in_region = himalayan_region
			}
		}
		area:suvarna_gotra_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_suvarna_gotra
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = suvarna_gotra_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = suvarna_gotra_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_suvarna_gotra
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = suvarna_gotra_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_suvarna_gotra
			days = 9125
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = suvarna_gotra_frontier_cost
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			days = 18250

				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "suvarna_gotra_area"
						adjective = "suvarna_gotra_area"
					}
					save_scope_as = suvarna_gotra_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:5566.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_kingdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:suvarna_gotra_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}

namespace = 11china_frontier

11china_frontier.100 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "china_frontier.100.t"	#陀罗钵底
	desc = "china_frontier.100.desc"
	picture = event_china_frontier_tropical
	goto_location = scope:dvaravati_frontier
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		capital_scope = {
			NOR = {
				is_in_region = suvarnabhumi_region
				is_in_region = funan_region
			}
		}
		area:dvaravati_area = {
			any_area_province = {
				owner = root
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = hold_dvaravati
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = dvaravati_area
					owner = root
				}
				save_scope_as = dvaravati_frontier
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.a"		#維持10年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_dvaravati
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = dvaravati_frontier_cost
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.b"		#維持25年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_dvaravati
			days = 9125
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = dvaravati_frontier_cost
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.c"		#維持50年
		set_variable = {
			name = hold_dvaravati
			days = 18250
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = dvaravati_frontier_cost
			duration = 18250
		}
		add_manpower = -10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -2.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.d"		#釋放朝貢
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_tributary_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:dvaravati_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "SUV"
						adjective = "SUV"
					}
					save_scope_as = dvaravati_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:9813.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_kingdom
				}
			}
			root = {
				make_subject = {
					target = scope:dvaravati_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = dvaravati_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:dvaravati_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "china_frontier.1.e"		#棄守
		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:dvaravati_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					name = {
						name = "SUV"
						adjective = "SUV"
					}
					save_scope_as = dvaravati_country_scope
					set_primary_culture = p:9813.culture 
	 				change_government = tribal_kingdom
				}
			}

				}

			}
		}

					target = scope:wuwei_country_scope
					type = tributary
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_in_area = wuwei_area
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:wuwei_country_scope
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		custom_tooltip = china_frontier_abandon_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:wuwei_frontier = {
				create_country = {
					save_scope_as = wuwei_country_scope
